#[CORVETTE] Fission Reactor
utility_component_template = {
	key = "CORVETTE_FISSION_REACTOR"
	size = small
	icon = "GFX_ship_part_ukn_reactor_1"
	icon_frame = 1
	power = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_power
	resources = {
		category = ship_components
		cost = {
			minerals = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_minerals
			alloys = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_alloys
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_ukn_meta_materials
#			ukn_femtomatter = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_ukn_femtomatter
#			ukn_condensics = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_ukn_condensics
#			ukn_quasi_matter = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_ukn_quasi_matter
#			ukn_causalitons = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_ukn_causalitons
#			exotic_gases = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_exotic_gases
#			rare_crystals = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_rare_crystals
#			volatile_motes = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_volatile_motes
#			ehof_sr_negative_mass = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_cost_ehof_sr_negative_mass
#---
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_armor_cost_ukn_meta_materials
#			nanites = @ukn_corvette_t1_armor_cost_nanites
#---
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_shields_cost_ukn_meta_materials
#			volatile_motes = @ukn_corvette_t1_shields_cost_volatile_motes
		}
		upkeep = {
#			energy = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_energy
			minerals = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_minerals
			alloys = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_alloys
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_ukn_meta_materials
#			ukn_femtomatter = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_ukn_femtomatter
#			ukn_condensics = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_ukn_condensics
#			ukn_quasi_matter = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_ukn_quasi_matter
#			ukn_causalitons = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_ukn_causalitons
#			exotic_gases = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_exotic_gases
#			volatile_motes = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_volatile_motes
#			sr_dark_matter = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_sr_dark_matter
#			ehof_sr_negative_mass = @ukn_corvette_t1_reactor_upkeep_ehof_sr_negative_mass
		}
	}

	prerequisites = { "tech_fission_power" }
	component_set = "power_core"
	size_restriction = { corvette colonizer lithoid_colonizer lithoid_colonizer sponsored_colonizer constructor science transport crisis_corvette }
	upgrades_to = "CORVETTE_FUSION_REACTOR"

	ai_weight = {
		weight = 1
	}
}
